                                13 ^{

                                    02=if(!ship) continue;
                                    03=if(ship == cur_ship) continue;
                                    04=ShipDeleteCustomShipInfo(ship, 'ShuMercs_QuestTargetAttackMark');
                                    05=RelationToRanger(ship, Player(), 0);
                                    06=RelationToRanger(GetShipHomePlanet(ship), Player(), 0);
                                    07=if(ShipInScript(ship, 0)) ShipOut(ship);
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                OnActCodeTypes=t_OnStep,t_OnTakingDamageEn,t_OnTakingDamageSp,t_OnTakingDamageMi
                OnActStepTypes=0
            }
            ShuMercs_QuestTargetAttackMark ^{
                Description=NoShow
                Icon=0
                Name=Автоматически выводит уведомление и портит отношение с напавшими наёмниками и игроком, в случае получения урона конкретной целью или кораблями её группы
                OnActCode ^{
                    01=dword ship = ScriptItemActShip();
                    02=dword attacker = ScriptItemActObject1();
                    03=if(ObjectType(attacker) == 7) attacker = MissileOwner(attacker);
                    04=if(!attacker) exit;
                    05=if(ObjectType(attacker) == 5)
                    06 ^{
                        01=if(ShipType(attacker) == 'PlayerMerc' || attacker == Player())
                        02 ^{
                            01=if(ShipInScript(attacker))
                            02 ^{
                                01=dword cur_info = CurInfo();
                                02=unknown GetParFromString = ImportedFunction('UtilityFunctions', 'GetParFromString');
                                03=str ships_id = ShipCustomShipInfoTextData(0, cur_info, 1);
                                04=dword head_ship = GetParFromString(ships_id, ',', 0, 0);
                                05=int check = (attacker == Player());
                                06=if(!check) check = (GetData(3, attacker) == head_ship);
                                07=if(check && head_ship)
                                08 ^{
                                    01=head_ship = IdToShip(head_ship);
                                    02=if(ShipStar(Player()) == ShipStar(head_ship) && ShipInNormalSpace(Player()))
                                    03 ^{
                                        01=if(Dist(Player(), head_ship) <= ShipRadarRange(Player()))
                                        02 ^{
                                            01=str ether_text = ShipCustomShipInfoTextData(0, cur_info, 2);
                                            02=if(ether_text != '')
                                            03 ^{
                                                01=str ether_icon = GetParFromString(ether_text, ',,,', 0, 0);
                                                02=int ether_type = GetParFromString(ether_text, ',,,', 1, 0);
                                                03=ether_text = Format(GetParFromString(ether_text, ',,,', 2, 0), '<ThisShip' + '>', Name(ship), '255,240,100');
                                                04=CustomEther(ether_icon, ether_type, '', ether_text, head_ship);
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                    04=ShipDeleteCustomShipInfo(head_ship, 'ShuMercs_QuestTargetAttackMark');
                                    05=RelationToRanger(head_ship, Player(), 0);
                                    06=unknown ParsCountFromString = ImportedFunction('UtilityFunctions', 'ParsCountFromString');
                                    07=str command_line = ShipCustomShipInfoTextData(0, cur_info, 3);
                                    08=int command_check = 0;
                                    09=if(ParsCountFromString(command_line, ',') > 4) command_check = 1;
                                    10=for(int i = 1; i < ParsCountFromString(ships_id, ','); i = i + 1)
                                    11 ^{
                                        01=ship = IdToShip(GetParFromString(ships_id, ',', i, 0));
                                        02=if(!ship) continue;
                                        03=ShipDeleteCustomShipInfo(ship, 'ShuMercs_QuestTargetAttackMark');
                                        04=RelationToRanger(ship, Player(), 0);
                                        05=if(command_check && command_line != '')
                                        06 ^{
                                            01=for(i = 0; i <= 3; i = i + 1)
                                            02 ^{
                                                01=SetData(0 + GetParFromString(command_line, ',', i, 0), i, ship);
                                            }
                                        }
                                    }
                                    12=if(!command_check && command_line != '')
                                    13 ^{
                                        01=for(i = 0; i <= 3; i = i + 1)
                                        02 ^{
                                            01=SetData(0 + GetParFromString(command_line, ',', i, 0), i, head_ship);
                                        }
                                    }
                                    14=dword offended_sector = GalaxySectors(ShipCustomShipInfoData(0, cur_info, 1) - 1);
                                    15=if(offended_sector) ConChangeRelationToRanger(offended_sector, Player(), -100);
                                    16=dword offended_planet = IdToPlanet(ShipCustomShipInfoData(0, cur_info, 2));
                                    17=if(offended_planet) RelationToRanger(offended_planet, Player(), 0);
                                    18=dword offended_ship = IdToPlanet(ShipCustomShipInfoData(0, cur_info, 3));
                                    19=if(offended_ship) RelationToRanger(offended_ship, Player(), 0);
                                }
                            }
                        }
                    }
                }
                OnActCodeTypes=t_OnTakingDamageEn,t_OnTakingDamageSp,t_OnTakingDamageMi
            }

                                    01=for(i = 1; i <= 5; i = i + 1)
                                    02 ^{
                                        01=if(ShipEqInSlot(cur_ship, t_Weapon1, i))
                                        02 ^{
                                            01=InterfaceText('Ship', 'GunBatteryLabelSlot' + i, 'x' + (attacks_count + 1));
                                            03=InterfaceState('Ship', 'GunBatteryLabelSlot' + i, 1);
                                        }
                                        03=else
                                        04 ^{
                                            01=InterfaceState('Ship', 'GunBatteryLabelSlot' + i, 0);
                                        }
                                    }
                                }
                                04=else
                                05 ^{
                                    01=for(i = 1; i <= 5; i = i + 1)
                                    02 ^{
                                        01=InterfaceState('Ship', 'GunBatteryLabelSlot' + i, 0);
                                    }
                                }
                            }
                        }
                        12=else
                        13 ^{
                            01=for(i = 1; i < ShipItems(cur_ship); i = i + 1)
                            02 ^{
                                01=item = ShipItems(cur_ship, i);
                                02=cost = ItemExtraSpecialsCountByType(item, bon_num);
                                03=if(!cost)
                                04 ^{
                                    01=NoDropItem(item, 1);
                                    02=continue;
                                }
                                05=ItemCost(item, cost);
                                06=ItemExtraSpecialsDeleteByType(item, bon_num, cost);
                            }
                            03=for(i = 0; i < ShipArts(cur_ship); i = i + 1)
                            04 ^{
                                01=item = ShipArts(cur_ship, i);
                                02=cost = ItemExtraSpecialsCountByType(item, bon_num);
                                03=if(!cost)
                                04 ^{
                                    01=NoDropItem(item, 1);
                                    02=continue;
                                }
                                05=ItemCost(item, cost);
                                06=ItemExtraSpecialsDeleteByType(item, bon_num, cost);
                            }
                            05=if(~ShipFindCustomShipInfoByType(cur_ship, 'TrancNPCOwnerInfo'))
                            06 ^{
                                08=item = CreateQuestItem('WeightReserve', 0);
                                09=ItemSize(item, 0);
                                10=AddItemToShip(cur_ship, item);
                                11=NoDropItem(item, 1);
                                12=ItemIsInUse(item, cur_ship, 1);
                            }
                            07=ArrangeItems(cur_ship);
                        }
                    }
                }
                OnActCodeTypes=t_OnEnteringForm,t_OnReEnteringForm,t_OnLeavingForm
            }
        }
    }
}
